## Page 4

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.73pt;color:#000000">仅供非商业用途或交流学</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.16pt;color:#000000">习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.57pt;color:#000000">使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:12.17pt;color:#000000">.· </span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.34pt;color:#000000">内容简介</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">本书是一本系统介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.49pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.55pt;color:#000000"> 语言编程的书籍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.60pt;color:#000000">。首</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">先介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.49pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000"> 语言的基础知识，使读者对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.41pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.53pt;color:#000000"> 语言有一个整</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">体的认知。接着围绕</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.22pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.22pt;color:#000000"> 语言的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.09pt;color:#000000">三大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">语言特性：类型系统、接口和并发展开论述，本书不单单介绍每个语</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.34pt;color:#000000">言特性怎么使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.90pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.41pt;color:#000000">在章节的最后还对重要语言特性的底层实现原理做了介绍。接着介绍反射这个高级语言</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">特征</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.64pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.47pt;color:#000000">此外，本书专门用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.34pt;color:#000000">一章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">的篇幅来介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.49pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000"> 语言的陆阱。最后介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.49pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.34pt;color:#000000"> 语言的工程实践和编程思想。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">相信本书能够帮助读者快速、深入地了解和学习这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.31pt;color:#000000">门</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.09pt;color:#000000">语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.50pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">本书适合各个层次的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.22pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000"> 语言开发者阅读，初学者可以系统地从头学习，有一定的编程经验者可以选</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.85pt;color:#000000">择性地阅读本书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000">未经许可，不得以任何方式复制或妙袭本书之部分或全部内容</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.18pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.42pt;color:#000000">版权所有，侵权必究</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.16pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.07pt;color:#000000">图书在版编目（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.88pt;color:#000000">CIP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.98pt;color:#000000"> ）数据</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.12pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.91pt;color:#000000"> 语言核</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.68pt;color:#000000">心</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">编程／李文塔著</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.27pt;color:#000000">．</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:13.19pt;color:#000000">写（乍背景</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.27pt;color:#000000">2007</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.76pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">言诞生于谷歌公司</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.76pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.31pt;color:#000000">2009</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000"> 年开源，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.31pt;color:#000000">2012</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 年推</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.03pt;color:#000000">出</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.44pt;color:#000000">1.0</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 版本</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.91pt;color:#000000">曾</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">两</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">次获得</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.66pt;color:#000000">TIO</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">BE </span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.08pt;color:#000000">年度语言（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">2009</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 年和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">2016</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 年</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.67pt;color:#000000">〕。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.40pt;color:#000000">2012</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000"> 年起</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.07pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">全球大量的开源项目开始使</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.78pt;color:#000000"> 语言进行开发，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.58pt;color:#000000">目前</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.13pt;color:#000000"> 语言已经成为云计算领域事实上的标准语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.13pt;color:#000000">特别是在容器领域</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">诞生了一大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">批</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">优秀</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.90pt;color:#000000">的开源软件，如</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Docker</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.64pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.22pt;color:#000000">2017</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 年区块链技术在国内大热，区块链两个大的技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">平台以太坊（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.31pt;color:#000000">Ethereum</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000"> ）和超级账本（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.41pt;color:#000000">Hyper</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">ledger</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000"> ）与项目</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.91pt;color:#000000">Fabric</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000"> 都是基</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000"> 语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">构</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">建</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.92pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color:#000000"> 语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">应</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">用领域</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">逐步</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">扩</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.81pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">目前在区块链</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">云</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">计</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">算</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.80pt;color:#000000">、中间</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">件和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">服</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">务器编</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">程领域显现出明</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">显</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">优</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">势</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000"> 语言最先在云</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">计</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">算公司盛行</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">随后大量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">互联</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">初创企业将</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 语言作为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">后台主要开</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">发语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">目前，无论</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">互联</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">公司里</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">独角兽</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color:#000000">，还</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">BAT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.79pt;color:#000000"> （百度、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">阿</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">里</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.36pt;color:#000000">巴巴、腾讯），</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">都己</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">将</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">作为其技术枝的重要组成部分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.64pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">市场对于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 语言编程人才的需求量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">也</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">持</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000">续上升</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">目前</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">言编程类图书有如下几</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">类</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">别</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.71pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">基础全面型</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">七牛团队写作</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000">翻译的几本书（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000"> 语言编程》《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000"> 程序设计语言》等）</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">，系</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">统地介绍了</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 开发的基础知识，为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.84pt;color:#000000"> 语言在国内的推广做出了很大的贡献。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">源码</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">深</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">入</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">型</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.77pt;color:#000000">《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.71pt;color:#000000"> 语言学习笔记》</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.70pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">上半部</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">分是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000"> 语言基</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">础</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">知识</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.28pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.80pt;color:#000000">总结</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">，下</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000">半部分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">源码进</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">是学</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.15pt;color:#000000">习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.02pt;color:#000000">内</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">部原理非常好</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">参考</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">书</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">专</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">业</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">领域型</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">专注于介绍某个应用领域，比如谢孟军的《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Web</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 编程</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">》</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.19pt;color:#000000">，这类图书主要是介绍使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">市面上</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000"> 语言的图书这么</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">多</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.91pt;color:#000000">了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.02pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000">为什么又要写</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">本，本书和市面上的图书有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">什</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">么区别呢？</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">也</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000">是我写这本书</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">之</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">前就认真思考过的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.92pt;color:#000000">问</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">题。我发现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">市</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">面上缺少介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000"> 语言核</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">心</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.91pt;color:#000000">特性和使用陷</span>

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.72pt;color:#000000">仅供非商业用途或交流学习佼用</span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">IV </span>
<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:12.00pt;color:#000000">I </span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.33pt;color:#000000"> 语言核</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">ω编程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.22pt;color:#000000">阱的书。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000"> 语言核心特性包括类型系统、接口、并发，这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.91pt;color:#000000">三部</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.85pt;color:#000000">分是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.72pt;color:#000000"> 语言最精华、最优美、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">最重要的语言特性。于是我就围绕这三个主题写了本书，书名就叫《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.86pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000"> 语言核心编程》。以类</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">型系统为例，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000"> 语言中的类型涉及简单类型、复合类型、命名类型、未命名类型、静态类型、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">动态类型、底层类型、接口类型</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.85pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.03pt;color:#000000">具体类型及类型字面量等诸多概念，这些在先前的书籍里没</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.03pt;color:#000000">有系统地介绍过，本书试图帮助读者梳理清楚这些类型的含义，建立概念，认清类型本质并学</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">会使用；在并发编程中给出了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 个并发编程范式并系统地介绍了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">co</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.75pt;color:#000000">ntext</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000"> 标准库，这也是本书特</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.12pt;color:#000000">有的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:14.66pt;color:#000000">内容简介</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">本书共</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 章，围绕如下主题展开：基础知识（第</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.92pt;color:#000000">l</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.68pt;color:#000000"> 章）、语言核</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">心</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.65pt;color:#000000">（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 章～第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.35pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000"> 章〉、工</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">程管理（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.85pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000"> 章）和编程哲学（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000"> 章）。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:13.41pt;color:#000000">基础知识</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">第</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.07pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000"> 语言编程的基础知识。基础知识部分力求从系统性的角度讲述</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000"> 语言简洁</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">的语法知识，试图帮助读者了解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">言源程序基本</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">结构，这是本书不同于其他书籍的地方。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">本章先对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000"> 的源程序进行整体介绍，然后从词法分析的角度介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 语言的各个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.84pt;color:#000000">t</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.49pt;color:#000000">oken</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000"> ，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">接着</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.08pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000"> 语言的基础语法：变</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000">和常量、数据类型及控制结构，让读者学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000"> 语言的语法知识</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.78pt;color:#000000">时可以“既见树木，又见森林”。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:13.52pt;color:#000000">语言核心</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000">本书的第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.53pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">～</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000"> 章讲解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000"> 语言核心知识，这部分是本书最核心、最重要的部分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000">主要围绕</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">如下</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000"> 个主题展开</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.55pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">类型系统</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">本书用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000"> 章的篇幅来讲解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.43pt;color:#000000"> 语言的类型系统，分别是第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.62pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000"> 章函数、第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000"> 章类型系统和第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.62pt;color:#000000">4</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.34pt;color:#000000">章接口。类型系统是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.08pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.82pt;color:#000000"> 语言的灵魂，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000"> 语言小而美的类型系统是其区别于其他语言的显著特</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">征。函数在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 语言中是“</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.19pt;color:#000000"> 一等公民</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">”，非侵入式的接口设计也很有特点。类型系统是本书的一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">条主要线索，几乎贯穿本书的所有章节，在反射章节里会对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000"> 的类型系统做一个总结。掌握</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">类型系统是写好</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.71pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.55pt;color:#000000"> 程序的关键。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.72pt;color:#000000">仅供非商业用途或交流学习使用</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.19pt;color:#000000">并发编程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.18pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.34pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000"> 并发编程，并发编程的原生支持是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.34pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000"> 语言显著的语言特征。“不要通过共</span>

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">享</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">内存来通信，而</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.03pt;color:#000000">通过通</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">信来共享</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.53pt;color:#000000">内存”，本章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">首先讲解语言层面对并发</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">的支持，接</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">着</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">讲解</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.91pt;color:#000000">反射</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">言反</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">射的相</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">关知</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">识</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">反射是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 语言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.19pt;color:#000000">高级特性</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">，反射是把“</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 双</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.69pt;color:#000000">刃剑”，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">用好</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.78pt;color:#000000">了会有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">强大的威力，但由于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">其复杂</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">性且易产生运行时</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.90pt;color:#000000">panic</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000"> ，因此反射</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.91pt;color:#000000">又表</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">现出脆弱性</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.64pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.78pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color:#000000">言没有提</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">供泛型支持，所以</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">在开发框架</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">和大型系统中反射</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">是必须面对的一个技术点</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">，市面</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">上的图书对这部分的介绍不多，本书分类总结了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000"> 的反射</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.66pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">，尽可能梳理出条理清晰的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.56pt;color:#000000">API</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">结构</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.95pt;color:#000000">；同时以</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.14pt;color:#000000">类型系统和接口底层实现为基础来介绍反射；最后介绍著名的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.17pt;color:#000000">We</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">b</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 框</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">架</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.78pt;color:#000000">martini</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.82pt;color:#000000">中使用的依赖注入库</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.34pt;color:#000000">inject</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.57pt;color:#000000"> 。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">陷阱和习惯用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">法</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">7</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.98pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.03pt;color:#000000">陷阱和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">一些习惯用法</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.56pt;color:#000000">，包括</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.91pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000"> 语言使用过程中容易</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.08pt;color:#000000">出错和初</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">学者容易</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.69pt;color:#000000">困惑的知识点。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.13pt;color:#000000"> 语言虽然设计简沽，但在某些方面还是有瑕疵的，比如</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.90pt;color:#000000">defe</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.12pt;color:#000000">r</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 陷阱、短变</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">量</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">声</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.34pt;color:#000000">明、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">range</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 临时变</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">量共享等。同时</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000"> 又有其鲜明的书写格式和习惯用法</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">，本</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">最后会介</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">绍这些内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:14.75pt;color:#000000">工程管理</span>
<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">Go </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">语言是一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.91pt;color:#000000">门</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">面向工程的语言，而不是学术界的产物，第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">8</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.90pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.88pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 语言工程管理方面</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.42pt;color:#000000">的知识，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">主要</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000">介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">编程环境、命名空</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">间和包</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">管理的相关内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:14.72pt;color:#000000">编程哲学</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.10pt;color:#000000">9</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">讨论编程哲</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">学，这部分内容不是介绍编程细节知识</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.96pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.92pt;color:#000000">读者可</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000">以把它当作散</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.25pt;color:#000000">文来读。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.04pt;color:#000000">先对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.38pt;color:#000000">G</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">o</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000"> 语言编程哲学做一个总结：少即是多，世界是并行的，组合优于继承，面</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000">向</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.47pt;color:#000000">接口编程，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.22pt;color:#000000">等等，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">试图从哲学的角度来阐述这些设计思想的先进性</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.26pt;color:#000000">。最后介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">的里程碑</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">事</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000">件及未</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000">来的发展方向。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:14.75pt;color:#000000">相关约定</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.01pt;color:#000000">本书使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 代表</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000"> 语言的简写，使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.27pt;color:#000000">go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 表示</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.10pt;color:#000000"> 语言的并发关键字，使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.76pt;color:#000000">routine</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> 代</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">表</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000"> 语言中的并发执行体</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">通道和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">ch</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">an</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 都</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">代表</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.89pt;color:#000000"> 语言的通信管道。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">切片和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.50pt;color:#000000">slice</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 都</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">表示</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Go</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">语言内置的可变数组。本书使用实例或者类型实例表示具体类型的变</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.09pt;color:#000000">，而没有使用传统</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">语言</span>
